     $(function () {
         var searchUrl = '/search/',
             $headerSearchInput = $('#CT_Header_0_ctl00_headerSearchInput'),
             $headerSearchBtn = $('#headerSearchBtn');
 
         $headerSearchInput.on("keypress", function(e) {
             if (e.which == 13) {
                 e.preventDefault();
                 $headerSearchBtn.trigger("click");
             }
         });
 
         $headerSearchBtn.on("click", function(e) {
             e.preventDefault();
             location.assign('' + searchUrl + '?keyword=' + encodeURIComponent($headerSearchInput.val()));
             return false;
         });
     });
     /* ]]> */

       <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
        /* <![CDATA[ */
 
     var dtCh = "-";
     var dteNow = new Date();
     var minYear = dteNow.getFullYear();
     var maxYear = minYear + 1;
 
     function isInteger(s) {
         var i;
         for (i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
             var c = s.charAt(i);
             if (((c < "0") || (c > "9"))) return false;
         }
         return true;
     }
 
     function stripCharsInBag(s, bag) {
         var i;
         var returnString = "";
         for (i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
             var c = s.charAt(i);
             if (bag.indexOf(c) == -1) returnString += c;
         }
         return returnString;
     }
 
     function daysInFebruary(year) {
         return (((year % 4 == 0) && ((!(year % 100 == 0)) || (year % 400 == 0))) ? 29 : 28);
     }
 
     function DaysArray(n) {
         for (var i = 1; i <= n; i++) {
             this[i] = 31
             if (i == 4 || i == 6 || i == 9 || i == 11) { this[i] = 30 }
             if (i == 2) { this[i] = 29 }
         }
         return this
     }
 
     function isDate(dtStr) {
         var daysInMonth = DaysArray(12)
         var pos1 = dtStr.indexOf(dtCh)
         var pos2 = dtStr.indexOf(dtCh, pos1 + 1)
         var strYear = dtStr.substring(0, pos1)
         var strMonth = dtStr.substring(pos1 + 1, pos2)
         var strDay = dtStr.substring(pos2 + 1)
         strYr = strYear
         if (strDay.charAt(0) == "0" && strDay.length > 1) strDay = strDay.substring(1)
         if (strMonth.charAt(0) == "0" && strMonth.length > 1) strMonth = strMonth.substring(1)
         for (var i = 1; i <= 3; i++) {
             if (strYr.charAt(0) == "0" && strYr.length > 1) strYr = strYr.substring(1)
         }
         month = parseInt(strMonth)
         day = parseInt(strDay)
         year = parseInt(strYr)
         if (pos1 == -1 || pos2 == -1) {
             alertPopup("Date is not in a valid format. Enter the date in mm/dd/yyyy format.", $(".quick-trip-planner"));
             return false
         }
         if (strMonth.length < 1 || month < 1 || month > 12) {
             alertPopup("Please enter a valid month.", $(".quick-trip-planner"));
             return false
         }
         if (strDay.length < 1 || day < 1 || day > 31 || (month == 2 && day > daysInFebruary(year)) || day > daysInMonth[month]) {
             alertPopup("Please enter a valid day.", $(".quick-trip-planner"));
             return false
         }
         if (strYear.length != 4 || year == 0 || year < minYear || year > maxYear) {
             var message = "Please enter a valid 4 digit year between " + minYear + " and " + maxYear + "."
             alertPopup(message, $(".quick-trip-planner"));
             return false
         }
         if (dtStr.indexOf(dtCh, pos2 + 1) != -1 || isInteger(stripCharsInBag(dtStr, dtCh)) == false) {
             alertPopup("Please enter a valid date.", $(".quick-trip-planner"));
             return false
         }
         return true
     }
 
 
     function submitGoogle() {
         var origAddress = $('#CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_origAddress').val();
         var destAddress = $('#CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_destAddress').val();
 
         if (origAddress == "" || destAddress == "") {
             alertPopup("Please fill out both the starting point and destination fields.", $(".quick-trip-planner"));
             return false;
         }
 
         if (pageTracker) pageTracker._trackPageview('/outgoing/www.google.com/transit');
 
         var drp = document.getElementById('CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_drpWhen');
         if (drp.value !== 'now') {
             var date = document.getElementById('CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_fdate');
             if (isDate(date.value) == false) {
                 date.focus();
                 return false;
             }
         }
         document.forms[0].target = '_blank';
         document.forms[0].action = location.href;
 
         $('#CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_hdnSubmitGoogle').click();
         document.forms[0].target = '';
         return false;
     }
 
 
     function submitMDV() {
         var origAddress = $('#CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_origAddress').val();
         var destAddress = $('#CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_destAddress').val();
 
         if (origAddress == "My location") {
             origAddress = $('#CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_hdnLatLngOrig').val() + ':WGS84';
             $("input[name=type_origin]").val("coord");
         };
         if (destAddress == "My location") {
             destAddress = $('#CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_hdnLatLngDest').val() + ':WGS84';
             $("input[name=type_destination]").val("coord");
         }
 
         if (origAddress == "" || destAddress == "") {
             alertPopup("Please fill out both the starting point and destination fields.", $(".quick-trip-planner"));
             return false;
         }
 
         $("#name_origin").val(encodeURIComponent(origAddress));
         $("#name_destination").val(encodeURIComponent(destAddress));
 
         var d = new Date();
         var itdDateDay = d.getDate();
         var itdDateMonth = d.getMonth() + 1;
         var itdDateYear = d.getFullYear();
         var itdTimeHour = d.getHours();
         var itdTimeMinute = d.getMinutes();
 
 
         var drp = document.getElementById('CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_drpWhen');
 
         if (drp.value !== 'now') {
             var sd = $("#CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_fdate").val();
             var arrsd = sd.split("-");
             itdDateMonth = arrsd[1];
             itdDateDay = arrsd[2];
             itdDateYear = arrsd[0];
 
             var arriveLeave = '';
             if (drp.value == 'arr') {
                 arriveLeave = document.getElementById('arriveLeave');
                 arriveLeave.value = 'arr'
             }
             if (drp.value == 'dep') {
                 arriveLeave = document.getElementById('arriveLeave');
                 arriveLeave.value = 'dep';
             }
             $("#itdTripDateTimeDepArr").val(arriveLeave.value);
 
             itdTimeHour = $("select[id*='ftime_H']").val();
             itdTimeMinute = $("select[id*='ftime_M']").val();
             itdTimeAMPM = $("select[id*='ftime_AMPM']").val();
 
 
             starttime24hr = convert_to_24h(itdTimeHour + ":" + itdTimeMinute + ":00 " + itdTimeAMPM)
             arrstarttime24hr = starttime24hr.split(":");
             itdTimeHour = arrstarttime24hr[0];
             itdTimeMinute = arrstarttime24hr[1];
         }
 
         $("#itdDateDay").val(itdDateDay);
         $("#itdDateMonth").val(itdDateMonth);
         $("#itdDateYear").val(itdDateYear);
 
         $("#itdTimeHour").val(itdTimeHour);
         $("#itdTimeMinute").val(itdTimeMinute);
 
         $("#std3_accesibilityNeededMacro").val($('#accessibility').prop('checked') * 1);
 
         $.ajax({
             type: 'GET',
             cache: false,
             url: '/ajax/keywordajax.aspx',
             dataType: 'json',
             async: false,
             data: { origAddress: origAddress, destAddress: destAddress },
             success: function (result) {
 
                 $("#name_origin").val(result.origAddress);
                 $("#name_destination").val(result.destAddress);
                 document.forms[0].action = $('#CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_lblLink').html()
                 document.forms[0].submit();
 
 
             }
         });
 
 
 
     }
 
     function convert_to_24h(time_str) {
         // Convert a string like 10:05:23 PM to 24h format, returns like [22,5,23]
         var time = time_str.match(/(\d+):(\d+):(\d+) (\w)/);
         var hours = Number(time[1]);
         var minutes = Number(time[2]);
         var seconds = Number(time[3]);
         var meridian = time[4].toLowerCase();
 
         if (meridian == 'p' && hours < 12) {
             hours = hours + 12;
         }
         else if (meridian == 'a' && hours == 12) {
             hours = hours - 12;
         }
         return hours + ":" + minutes;
     };
 
     function enterPressed(e) {
         var code;
         if (!e) var e = window.event;
 
         if (e.keyCode) {
             code = e.keyCode
         } else if (e.which) {
             code = e.which
         }
 
         if (code == 13) {
             var $target = $(e.target);
 
             if ( !$target.is("a") && !$target.is("button") ) {
                 alertPopup('Please choose a trip planner to get directions from.', $(".quick-trip-planner"));
                 return false;
 
             }
         }
     }
 
     function toggleGoogleDirections(checked) {
         if (checked) {
             $('#CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_btnGoogle').prop('disabled', true).attr("aria-disabled", "true");
         } else {
             $('#CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_btnGoogle').prop('disabled', false).attr("aria-disabled", "false");
         }
     }
 
     $(document).ready(function () {
 
         $("#CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_origAddress, #CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_destAddress").keyup(function (e) {
             $(this).removeClass("success");
             $(this).siblings("a").removeClass("detect-location-success");
         });
 
         $("#tpexpanderbtn").click(function (eo) {
             $("#tpexpoptions").slideDown(250, function () {
                 $("#tpexpanderarrow").css("backgroundImage", "url(/cms/images/tt_optpanel_rollup.gif)");
             });
             $("#tpexpanderbtn").unbind("click").animate({ opacity: 0 }, 250, "swing", function () {
                 $(this).hide();
             });
         });
 
         $('#CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_drpWhen').change(function () {
             if (this.value == 'dep' || this.value == 'arr') {
                 $('#div-hide-and-show').show().addClass("active");
             } else {
                 $('#div-hide-and-show').hide().removeClass("active");
             }
         });
 
         if (!Modernizr.inputtypes.date) {
             $("#CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_fdate").datepicker({
                 dateFormat: 'yy-mm-dd'
             });
             $("#CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_fdate").datepicker("setDate", new Date());
         } else {
             var $fdate = $("#CT_QuickTripPlanner_0_fdate"),
                 dt = new Date(),
                 mm = dt.getMonth() + 1,
                 dd = dt.getDate(),
                 year = dt.getFullYear();
 
             $fdate.val([year, (mm > 9 ? '' : '0') + mm, (dd > 9 ? '' : '0') + dd].join('-'));
         }
 
         var tpOptions = new Object();
         if (!navigator.geolocation) {
             $('.detect-location').hide();
         } else {
             tpOptions.enableHighAccuracy = true;
             tpOptions.timeout = 10000;
             tpOptions.maximumAge = 10000;
         }
 
         var clickedEl = null;
         $('.detect-location').click(function (e) {
             e.preventDefault();
 
             clickedEl = $(this);
             navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(tpSuccess, tpError, tpOptions);
             clickedEl.addClass("loading");
         });
 
         function tpSuccess(position) {
             var coords = position.coords;
             clickedEl.removeClass("loading");
             if (coords.accuracy > parseInt('1500')) {
                 clickedEl.siblings(".detect-location-error").show().focus();
                 if (!clickedEl.hasClass('detect-location-error'))
                     clickedEl.hide();
                 alertPopup("Specific location not detected", $(".quick-trip-planner"));
             } else {
                 clickedEl.addClass("detect-location-success");
                 $(clickedEl.attr('target')).val('My location');
                 $(clickedEl.attr('target')).addClass("success");
                 $(clickedEl.attr('target2')).val(parseFloat(coords.longitude.toFixed(5)) + ':' + parseFloat(coords.latitude.toFixed(5)));
             }
         }
 
         function tpError(pe) {
             coords = null;
             clickedEl.removeClass("loading");
             clickedEl.siblings(".detect-location-error").show().focus();
             if (!clickedEl.hasClass('detect-location-error'))
                 clickedEl.hide();
 
             alertPopup("Specific location not detected", $(".quick-trip-planner"));
         }
     });

             //setTimeout('loadHSJS();',1500)
             loadHSJS();
 
         });
 
         function loadHSJS() {
 
             if (typeof HawkSearch.suggestInit != "function") {
 
 
                 //if the homepage, include the autosuggest include only
                 if (window.location.pathname != '/') {
                     var newscript = document.createElement("script");
                     newscript.async = true;
                     //                alert(window.location.pathname);
                     //if the homepage, include the autosuggest include, otherwise the full hs include
                     newscript.src = HawkSearch.TrackingUrl + "/includes/hawksearch.min.js";
 
                     var s0 = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
                     //Created out of the flow of the document, 
                     //so the script file is downloaded and executed without waiting for HTML rendering.
                     s0.parentNode.insertBefore(newscript, s0);
                 }
 
                 //Cache enabled and loaded asynchronously 
                 var newscript = document.createElement("script");
                 newscript.async = true;
                 newscript.src = HawkSearch.TrackingUrl + "/includes/hawksuggester.min.js";
                 var s0 = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
                 s0.parentNode.insertBefore(newscript, s0);
 
                 
                 
             }

                     hiddenDivName: '',
                     isAutoWidth: false
                 });
                     
                         HawkSearch.suggestInit('#CT_Header_0_ctl01_txtSearch',
                 {
                             lookupUrlPrefix: HawkSearch.TrackingUrl + '/?fn=ajax&f=GetSuggestions',
                     hiddenDivName: '',
                     isAutoWidth: false
                 });
                     
             };
